/**************************************************** * Web Entry ****************************************************/ function doGet(e) { e = e || {}; const p = e.parameter || {}; const mode = String(p.mode || "").toLowerCase(); } if (!action) { return outputJson_({ ok: true, version: "V76.0", message: "MES Apps Script API Ready", time: now_() }, callback); } let result; try { result = handleGetAction_(action, p); } catch (err) { result = { ok: false, version: "V76.0", action: action, message: String(err && err.message ? err.message : err), stack: String(err && err.stack ? err.stack : "") }; log_("GET_ERROR", action + "｜" + result.message); } return outputJson_(result, callback); } function doPost(e) { e = e || {}; const p = e.parameter || {}; const action = String(p.action || "").toLowerCase(); } } catch (err) { result = { ok: false, version: "V76.0", action: action, message: String(err && err.message ? err.message : err) }; log_("POST_ERROR", action + "｜" + result.message); } return outputJson_(result, p.callback || ""); }); } /**************************************************** * V92 Shared Data Engine｜Phase 1（後端新增、前端尚未切換） * * 設計原則： * 1) 不修改任何既有 API 行為。 * 2) 優先讀取 Target_Order_Cache；沒有資料時才退回 source_data。 * 3) 採分頁回傳，避免單次 payload 過大。 * 4) CacheService 只快取小型狀態、查詢結果及可安全容納的分頁。 * 5) 提供 cache clear，供 ERP 更新完成後主動失效。 ****************************************************/ const SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION = "V92.5-LOOKUP2"; const SHARED_CACHE_PREFIX = "MES_SHARED_V921_"; const SHARED_CACHE_TTL_STATUS = 60; const SHARED_CACHE_TTL_PAGE = 120; const SHARED_CACHE_TTL_LOOKUP = 300; const SHARED_CACHE_SAFE_BYTES = 85000; function sharedDataStatus_(p) { p = p || {}; if (cached) { try { const obj = JSON.parse(cached); obj.cache_hit = true; return obj; } catch (ignore) {} } } const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const names = [ SHEET_SOURCE, SHEET_TARGET_CACHE, SHEET_KEYIN, SHEET_TARGET, SHEET_APS_WORKPOOL, SHEET_APS_SCHEDULE, SHEET_APS_SPEED, SHEET_APS_MACHINE, SHEET_SPEED_FEEDBACK, SHEET_43, SHEET_PD11B, SHEET_SL31A, SHEET_5C, SHEET_53, V78_SHEET_91, V78_SHEET_93, V78_SHEET_39 ]; const sheets = {}; names.forEach(function(name) { const sh = ss.getSheetByName(name); sheets[name] = sh ? { exists: true, rows: Math.max(0, sh.getLastRow() - 1), columns: sh.getLastColumn() } : { exists: false, rows: 0, columns: 0 }; }); const preferred = sheets[SHEET_TARGET_CACHE] && sheets[SHEET_TARGET_CACHE].rows > 0 ? SHEET_TARGET_CACHE : SHEET_SOURCE; const result = { ok: true, version: SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION, action: "sharedstatus", engine: "Shared Data Engine Phase 1", preferred_source: preferred, preferred_rows: sheets[preferred] ? sheets[preferred].rows : 0, sheets: sheets, cache_hit: false, time: now_() }; sharedCachePutSafe_(cache, cacheKey, result, SHARED_CACHE_TTL_STATUS); return result; } function sharedDataBootstrap_(p) { p = p || {}; const started = Date.now(); const offset = Math.max(0, Number(p.offset || 0)); const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || 200), 1), 500); const sourceRequested = normalizeSharedSource_(p.source || ""); const sourceSheet = sourceRequested || sharedPreferredSourceSheet_(); obj.elapsed_ms = Date.now() - started; return obj; } catch (ignore) {} } } const page = sharedReadSheetPage_(sourceSheet, offset, limit); const normalized = page.rows.map(function(row) { return sharedNormalizeRow_(row, sourceSheet); }).filter(function(row) { return row.work_order_no || row.order_no || row.command_no || row.report_no || row.batch_no || row.part_no; }); const result = { ok: true, version: SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION, action: "sharedbootstrap", source: sourceSheet, offset: offset, limit: limit, read: page.rows.length, count: normalized.length, total: page.total, next_offset: Math.min(page.total, offset + page.rows.length), done: offset + page.rows.length >= page.total, fingerprint: fingerprint, rows: normalized, cache_hit: false, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started, time: now_() }; sharedCachePutSafe_(cache, cacheKey, result, SHARED_CACHE_TTL_PAGE); return result; } function sharedDataLookup_(p) { p = p || {}; const started = Date.now(); const rawQuery = String( p.q || p.query || p.key || p.work_order_no || p.order_no || p.command_no || p.report_no || p.batch_no || p.part_no || "" ).trim(); const query = sharedNormalizeKey_(rawQuery); if (!query) { return { ok: false, version: SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION, action: "sharedlookup", message: "缺少查詢條件 q", rows: [] }; } const exact = String(p.exact || "1") !== "0"; const maxResults = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || 30), 1), 100); const sourceRequested = normalizeSharedSource_(p.source || ""); const sources = sourceRequested ? [sourceRequested] : sharedLookupSourceOrder_(); const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); const sourceFingerprint = sources.map(sharedSheetFingerprint_).join("__"); const cacheKey = SHARED_CACHE_PREFIX + "LOOKUP2_" + sourceFingerprint + "_" + (exact ? "E_" : "F_") + sharedCacheKeyToken_(query) + "_" + maxResults; const cached = cache.get(cacheKey); if (cached) { try { const obj = JSON.parse(cached); obj.cache_hit = true; obj.elapsed_ms = Date.now() - started; return obj; } catch (ignore) {} } const matches = []; const searchedSources = []; const sourceCounts = {}; const seen = {}; for (let s = 0; s < sources.length && matches.length < maxResults; s++) { const sheetName = sources[s]; const found = sharedFindRowsFast_(sheetName, rawQuery, query, exact, maxResults - matches.length); searchedSources.push(sheetName); sourceCounts[sheetName] = found.length; for (let i = 0; i < found.length && matches.length < maxResults; i++) { const n = sharedNormalizeRow_(found[i], sheetName); const dedupeKey = sharedResultDedupeKey_(n); if (seen[dedupeKey]) continue; seen[dedupeKey] = true; matches.push(n); } // 精準查詢只要優先來源已找到完整資料，就不再掃後續大型工作表。 if (exact && matches.length > 0 && sharedRowsHavePrimaryIdentity_(matches)) break; } const result = { ok: true, version: SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION, action: "sharedlookup", engine: "Shared Lookup Engine 2.0", source: searchedSources.join("+"), sources_searched: searchedSources, source_counts: sourceCounts, query: query, raw_query: rawQuery, exact: exact, count: matches.length, rows: matches, fingerprint: sourceFingerprint, cache_hit: false, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started, time: now_() }; sharedCachePutSafe_(cache, cacheKey, result, SHARED_CACHE_TTL_LOOKUP); return result; } /** * V92.5 Shared Lookup Engine 2.0 * 優先順序：Target_Order_Cache → source_data → 八份 ERP 原始工作表。 * 使用 TextFinder 直接定位儲存格，避免每次 readSheetRows_ 掃描數萬筆。 */ function sharedLookupSourceOrder_() { const list = [ SHEET_TARGET_CACHE, SHEET_SOURCE, SHEET_43, SHEET_PD11B, SHEET_SL31A, SHEET_5C, SHEET_53, V78_SHEET_91, V78_SHEET_93, V78_SHEET_39 ]; const out = []; const seen = {}; list.forEach(function(name) { name = String(name || "").trim(); if (!name || seen[name]) return; seen[name] = true; out.push(name); }); return out; } function sharedFindRowsFast_(sheetName, rawQuery, normalizedQuery, exact, limit) { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName); if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() <= 1 || sh.getLastColumn() <= 0 || limit <= 0) return []; const lastCol = sh.getLastColumn(); const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0].map(function(h) { return String(h || "").trim(); }); const rowNumbers = []; const rowSeen = {}; const queryVariants = sharedLookupQueryVariants_(rawQuery, normalizedQuery); for (let q = 0; q < queryVariants.length && rowNumbers.length < limit; q++) { const variant = queryVariants[q]; if (!variant) continue; try { const finder = sh.getDataRange() .createTextFinder(variant) .matchCase(false) .matchEntireCell(!!exact) .useRegularExpression(false); const cells = finder.findAll() || []; for (let i = 0; i < cells.length && rowNumbers.length < limit; i++) { const rowNo = cells[i].getRow(); if (rowNo <= 1 || rowSeen[rowNo]) continue; rowSeen[rowNo] = true; rowNumbers.push(rowNo); } } catch (err) { log_("SHARED_LOOKUP_TEXTFINDER_WARN", sheetName + "｜" + String(err)); } } if (!rowNumbers.length) return []; rowNumbers.sort(function(a, b) { return a - b; }); const rows = []; rowNumbers.slice(0, limit).forEach(function(rowNo) { const vals = sh.getRange(rowNo, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0]; const obj = {}; headers.forEach(function(h, i) { if (!h) return; let v = vals[i]; if (v instanceof Date) v = Utilities.formatDate(v, TZ, "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"); obj[h] = v; }); rows.push(obj); }); return rows; } function sharedLookupQueryVariants_(rawQuery, normalizedQuery) { const variants = []; function add(v) { v = String(v || "").trim(); if (!v || variants.indexOf(v) >= 0) return; variants.push(v); } add(rawQuery); add(String(rawQuery || "").toUpperCase()); add(normalizedQuery); // 工單固定 12 碼時，同時嘗試標準化後的 12 碼。 if (/^[A-Z]{1,4}\d{8,}$/.test(normalizedQuery)) add(normalizedQuery.slice(0, 12)); return variants; } function sharedResultDedupeKey_(r) { r = r || {}; return [ sharedNormalizeKey_(r.work_order_no), sharedNormalizeKey_(r.command_no), sharedNormalizeKey_(r.order_no), sharedNormalizeKey_(r.report_no), sharedNormalizeKey_(r.batch_no), sharedNormalizeKey_(r.part_no), sharedNormalizeKey_(r.source) ].join("|"); } function sharedRowsHavePrimaryIdentity_(rows) { return (rows || []).some(function(r) { return !!( sharedNormalizeKey_(r.work_order_no) || sharedNormalizeKey_(r.command_no) || sharedNormalizeKey_(r.order_no) || sharedNormalizeKey_(r.report_no) || sharedNormalizeKey_(r.batch_no) ); }); } function sharedDataCacheClear_(p) { p = p || {}; const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(5000)) { return { ok: false, version: SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION, action: "sharedcacheclear", message: "快取正在由其他程序處理，請稍後再試" }; } try { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); const oldVersion = Number(props.getProperty("MES_SHARED_CACHE_EPOCH") || 0); const newVersion = oldVersion + 1; props.setProperty("MES_SHARED_CACHE_EPOCH", String(newVersion)); CacheService.getScriptCache().remove(SHARED_CACHE_PREFIX + "STATUS"); return { ok: true, version: SHARED_ENGINE_VERSION, action: "sharedcacheclear", cache_epoch: newVersion, message: "Shared Data Engine 快取版本已更新", time: now_() }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function sharedPreferredSourceSheet_() { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const cacheSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_TARGET_CACHE); if (cacheSheet && cacheSheet.getLastRow() > 1) return SHEET_TARGET_CACHE; return SHEET_SOURCE; } function normalizeSharedSource_(value) { const v = String(value || "").trim().toLowerCase(); if (!v) return ""; if (v === "target" || v === "targetcache" || v === "target_order_cache") return SHEET_TARGET_CACHE; if (v === "source" || v === "source_data") return SHEET_SOURCE; return ""; } function sharedReadSheetPage_(sheetName, offset, limit) { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName); if (!sh) return { rows: [], total: 0 }; const lastRow = sh.getLastRow(); const lastCol = sh.getLastColumn(); const total = Math.max(0, lastRow - 1); if (total <= 0 || lastCol <= 0 || offset >= total) return { rows: [], total: total }; const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0].map(function(h) { return String(h || "").trim(); }); const readCount = Math.min(limit, total - offset); const values = sh.getRange(offset + 2, 1, readCount, lastCol).getValues(); const rows = values.map(function(vals) { const obj = {}; headers.forEach(function(h, i) { if (h) obj[h] = vals[i]; }); return obj; }); return { rows: rows, total: total }; } function sharedSheetFingerprint_(sheetName) { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName); const epoch = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty("MES_SHARED_CACHE_EPOCH") || "0"; if (!sh) return "missing_" + epoch; return [sheetName, sh.getLastRow(), sh.getLastColumn(), epoch].join("_"); } function sharedNormalizeRow_(r, sourceSheet) { r = r || {}; const wo = wo12_(pick_(r, ["work_order_no","work_order","工單號","工單","工單編號","工令單號","製令單號","命令單號","命令單","WO"])); const orderNo = pick_(r, ["order_no","訂單單號","訂單號","客戶訂單","銷售單號","單號"]); const commandNo = pick_(r, ["command_no","命令單號","命令單","製令單號","製令","工令單號"]); const reportNo = pick_(r, ["report_no","daily_report_no","日報號","部門日報號","生產日報號"]); const batchNo = pick_(r, ["batch_no","生產批號","批號","製號","Lot","LOT","lot"]); const partNo = pick_(r, ["part_no","料號","品號","料品編號","產品料號","產品編號"]); return { source: pick_(r, ["source"]) || sourceSheet || "", work_order_no: wo, order_no: String(orderNo || "").trim(), command_no: String(commandNo || "").trim(), report_no: String(reportNo || "").trim(), batch_no: String(batchNo || "").trim(), part_no: String(partNo || "").trim(), input_part_no: String(pick_(r, ["input_part_no","投入料號","投入品號"]) || "").trim(), output_part_no: String(pick_(r, ["output_part_no","產出料號","產出品號"]) || "").trim(), input_lot_no: String(pick_(r, ["input_lot_no","投入製號","投入批號"]) || "").trim(), output_lot_no: String(pick_(r, ["output_lot_no","產出製號","產出批號"]) || "").trim(), customer: String(pick_(r, ["customer","customer_name","客戶","客戶名稱","客戶別"]) || "").trim(), product_spec: String(pick_(r, ["product_spec","spec","規格","產品規格","品名規格"]) || "").trim(), process: String(pick_(r, ["process","process_site","製程","站點","加工站點"]) || "").trim(), machine: String(pick_(r, ["machine","machine_code","機台","機台編號","設備編號"]) || "").trim().toUpperCase(), target_qty: pick_(r, ["target_qty","target_roll","預計產量","目標量","數量"]), target_unit: String(pick_(r, ["target_unit","unit","單位"]) || "").trim(), plan_date: dateKey_(pick_(r, ["plan_date","排程日期","計畫日期","預計生產日"])), due_date: dateKey_(pick_(r, ["due_date","預交日","預計交期","交期","交貨日"])), status: String(pick_(r, ["status","狀態","工單狀態"]) || "").trim(), updated_at: pick_(r, ["updated_at","更新時間","最後更新時間"]) }; } function sharedNormalizeKey_(value) { return String(value === null || value === undefined ? "" : value) .trim() .toUpperCase() .replace(/[\s\-_/\\.]/g, ""); } function sharedCacheKeyToken_(value) { const s = sharedNormalizeKey_(value); let hash = 2166136261; for (let i = 0; i < s.length; i++) { hash ^= s.charCodeAt(i); hash = Math.imul(hash, 16777619); } return (hash >>> 0).toString(36); } function sharedCachePutSafe_(cache, key, value, ttl) { try { const json = JSON.stringify(value); if (Utilities.newBlob(json).getBytes().length <= SHARED_CACHE_SAFE_BYTES) { cache.put(key, json, ttl); return true; } } catch (err) { log_("SHARED_CACHE_WARN", String(err && err.message ? err.message : err)); } return false; } /**************************************************** * Target Cache ****************************************************/ function targetCacheBuildStart_(p) { const sh = ensureSheet_(SHEET_TARGET_CACHE, TARGET_CACHE_HEADERS); clearDataKeepHeader_(sh, TARGET_CACHE_HEADERS); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sheets = targetAllowedSheets_().map(function(name) { const s = ss.getSheetByName(name); return { sheet: name, count: s ? Math.max(0, s.getLastRow() - 1) : 0 }; }); log_("targetCacheBuildStart", JSON.stringify(sheets)); return { ok: true, version: "V76.0", action: "targetcachebuildstart", sheets: sheets, time: now_() }; } function targetCacheBuildChunk_(p) { p = p || {}; const sheetName = normalizeSheetName_(p.sheet || p.sheetName || ""); if (targetAllowedSheets_().indexOf(sheetName) < 0) { throw new Error("不允許建立快取的工作表：" + sheetName); } const offset = Math.max(0, Number(p.offset || 0)); const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || 80), 1), 150); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const src = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName); if (!src) { return { ok: true, version: "V76.0", action: "targetcachebuildchunk", sheet: sheetName, read: 0, written: 0, next_offset: offset, done: true, total: 0, time: now_() }; } const lastRow = src.getLastRow(); const lastCol = src.getLastColumn(); const total = Math.max(0, lastRow - 1); if (offset >= total || total <= 0 || lastCol <= 0) { return { ok: true, version: "V76.0", action: "targetcachebuildchunk", sheet: sheetName, read: 0, written: 0, next_offset: total, done: true, total: total, time: now_() }; } const headers = src.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0].map(function(h) { return String(h || "").trim(); }); const rowsToRead = Math.min(limit, total - offset); const vals = src.getRange(offset + 2, 1, rowsToRead, lastCol).getValues(); const now = now_(); const out = []; vals.forEach(function(rowVals) { const obj = {}; headers.forEach(function(h, i) { if (h) obj[h] = rowVals[i]; }); const n = normalizeTargetRawRow_(obj, sheetName, rowVals, now); if (!n.work_order_no && !n.order_no && !n.part_no && !n.batch_no && !n.product_spec) return; out.push(TARGET_CACHE_HEADERS.map(function(h) { return n[h] !== undefined && n[h] !== null ? n[h] : ""; })); }); if (out.length) { const cache = ensureSheet_(SHEET_TARGET_CACHE, TARGET_CACHE_HEADERS); appendValues_(cache, out); } const next = offset + rowsToRead; return { ok: true, version: "V76.0", action: "targetcachebuildchunk", sheet: sheetName, read: rowsToRead, written: out.length, next_offset: next, done: next >= total, total: total, time: now_() }; } function targetCacheProgress_(p) { const sh = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(SHEET_TARGET_CACHE); const count = sh ? } function buildSpecMap_(slRows) { const map = {}; (slRows || []).forEach(function(r) { const keys = [r.work_order_no, r.order_no, r.part_no, r.batch_no].map(norm_).filter(Boolean); keys.forEach(function(k) { if (!map[k]) map[k] = r; const minSamples = Math.max(1, Number(p.min_samples || p.minSamples || 1)); const limit = Math.min(1000, Math.max(1, Number(p.limit || 300))); const rows = readSheetRows_(SHEET_MACHINE_USAGE); const groups = {}; function cleanProcess_(v) { return String(v || "").split("/")[0].trim(); } function widthFromSpec_(v) { const s = String(v || "").replace(/，/g, ","); // 優先抓「寬度mm」或乘號前後的 mm 尺寸；無法判斷時留空，避免錯學。 const patterns = [ /(?:寬|WIDTH)\s*[:：]?\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*MM/i, /(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*MM\s*[×X*]/i, /[×X*]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*MM/i, /(?:^|[^\d])(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*MM(?:[^\d]|$)/i ]; for (let i = 0; i < patterns.length; i++) { const m = s.match(patterns[i]); if (m) return Number(m[1]); } return 0; } function layerKey_(parts) { return parts.map(function(x){return norm_(x || "");}).join("||"); } function addMachine_(map, machine, source, date) { if (!map[machine]) map[machine] = {machine:machine,count:0,keyin_count:0,target_count:0,last_date:""}; const m = map[machine]; m.count++; if (source.indexOf("key") >= 0) m.keyin_count++; else if (source.indexOf("target") >= 0) m.target_count++; if (date && date > m.last_date) m.last_date = date; } rows.forEach(function(r) { const machine = String(r.machine_code || r.machine || "").trim().toUpperCase(); const identity = part || spec || workOrder; if (!identity) return; const width = widthFromSpec_(spec); const key = [identity, process].join("||"); if (!groups[key]) groups[key] = { key:key, part_no:part, product_spec:spec, process:process, width_mm:width, total_samples:0,target_samples:0,keyin_samples:0,last_used_date:"",machines:{},work_orders:{} }; // 建立四層經驗池：同料號、同規格、同寬度、同製程。 const pools = {part:{},spec:{},width:{},process:{}}; rows.forEach(function(r){ const machine=String(r.machine_code||r.machine||"").trim().toUpperCase(); if(!machine)return; const part=String(r.part_no||"").trim().toUpperCase(); const spec=String(r.product_spec||"").trim(); const process=cleanProcess_(r.process_site||r.process||""); const width=widthFromSpec_(spec); const source=String(r.source||"").toLowerCase(); const d=dateKey_(r.usage_date||r.created_at||""); const defs=[ ["part",part&&process?layerKey_([part,process]):""], ["spec",spec&&process?layerKey_([spec,process]):""], ["width",width&&process?layerKey_([width,process]):""], ["process",process?layerKey_([process]):""] ]; defs.forEach(function(def){ const kind=def[0],key=def[1];if(!key)return; if(!pools[kind][key])pools[kind][key]={samples:0,machines:{}}; pools[kind][key].samples++; addMachine_(pools[kind][key].machines,machine,source,d); }); }); function reliability_(n, scale) { if (!n) return 0; return Math.min(1, Math.log(n + 1) / Math.log(scale + 1)); } function layerShare_(pool, machine) { if (!pool || !pool.samples) return 0; return Number((pool.machines[machine] || {}).count || 0) / pool.samples; } const out = Object.keys(groups).map(function(k) { const g=groups[k]; const partPool=pools.part[layerKey_([g.part_no,g.process])] || null; const specPool=pools.spec[layerKey_([g.product_spec,g.process])] || null; const widthPool=g.width_mm ? (pools.width[layerKey_([g.width_mm,g.process])] || null) : null; const processPool=pools.process[layerKey_([g.process])] || null; const candidates={}; [partPool,specPool,widthPool,processPool].forEach(function(pool){ if(pool)Object.keys(pool.machines).forEach(function(m){candidates[m]=true;}); }); Object.keys(g.machines).forEach(function(m){candidates[m]=true;}); const scores=Object.keys(candidates).map(function(machine){ const partScore=35*layerShare_(partPool,machine)*reliability_(partPool?partPool.samples:0,8); const specScore=30*layerShare_(specPool,machine)*reliability_(specPool?specPool.samples:0,12); const widthScore=20*layerShare_(widthPool,machine)*reliability_(widthPool?widthPool.samples:0,20); const processScore=15*layerShare_(processPool,machine)*reliability_(processPool?processPool.samples:0,30); return {machine:machine,score:partScore+specScore+widthScore+processScore, exact_count:Number((g.machines[machine]||{}).count||0), last_date:String((g.machines[machine]||{}).last_date||"")}; }).sort(function(a,b){return b.score-a.score || b.exact_count-a.exact_count || b.last_date.localeCompare(a.last_date);}); const primary=scores[0]||{machine:"",score:0,exact_count:0}; const totalScore=scores.reduce(function(s,x){return s+x.score;},0); const dominance=totalScore?primary.score/totalScore*100:0; const evidenceSamples=(partPool?partPool.samples:0)+(specPool?specPool.samples:0)+(widthPool?widthPool.samples:0); const maturity=Math.min(1,0.48+Math.log(evidenceSamples+1)/Math.log(30)*0.52); const confidence=Math.max(1,Math.min(99,Math.round(dominance*maturity))); const shared=scores.slice(1).filter(function(x){return x.score>=8 && x.score>=primary.score*0.20;}); let status="待累積"; if(evidenceSamples>=12 && confidence>=78)status="高信心建議"; else if(evidenceSamples>=4 && confidence>=58)status="AI 建議"; const reasons=[]; reasons.push("同料號 "+Number(partPool?partPool.samples:0)+" 筆"); reasons.push("同規格 "+Number(specPool?specPool.samples:0)+" 筆"); reasons.push(g.width_mm ? ("同寬度 "+g.width_mm+"mm："+Number(widthPool?widthPool.samples:0)+" 筆") : "寬度未辨識"); reasons.push("同製程 "+Number(processPool?processPool.samples:0)+" 筆"); const basis="料號35%＋規格30%＋寬度20%＋製程15%；推薦 "+primary.machine+"，綜合得分 "+primary.score.toFixed(1); const exactMachines=Object.keys(g.machines).map(function(m){return g.machines[m];}) .sort(function(a,b){return b.count-a.count||String(b.last_date).localeCompare(String(a.last_date));}); return { learning_key:g.key,part_no:g.part_no,product_spec:g.product_spec,process:g.process,width_mm:g.width_mm||0, primary_machine:primary.machine,primary_count:primary.exact_count, shared_machines:shared.map(function(x){return x.machine;}).join(","),machine_count:scores.length, total_samples:g.total_samples,target_samples:g.target_samples,keyin_samples:g.keyin_samples, work_order_count:Object.keys(g.work_orders).length, same_part_samples:Number(partPool?partPool.samples:0),same_spec_samples:Number(specPool?specPool.samples:0), same_width_samples:Number(widthPool?widthPool.samples:0),same_process_samples:Number(processPool?processPool.samples:0), confidence:confidence,status:status,evidence_reason:reasons.join("｜"),recommendation_basis:basis, last_used_date:g.last_used_date,machine_detail:exactMachines, scored_machine_detail:scores }; }).filter(function(r){return r.total_samples>=minSamples;}) .sort(function(a,b){return b.confidence-a.confidence||b.total_samples-a.total_samples;}).slice(0,limit); const speedRows=readSheetRows_(SHEET_SPEED_FEEDBACK); out.forEach(function(r){ const matched=speedRows.filter(function(s){ const samePart=norm_(s.part||s.part_no||"")&&norm_(s.part||s.part_no||"")===norm_(r.part_no||""); const sameSpec=!samePart&&norm_(s.name||s.product_spec||"")&&norm_(s.name||s.product_spec||"")===norm_(r.product_spec||""); const sameProc=!r.process||norm_(s.process||s.process_site||"").indexOf(norm_(r.process))>=0; const sameMachine=!r.primary_machine||norm_(s.machine||s.machine_code||"")===norm_(r.primary_machine); return (samePart||sameSpec)&&sameProc&&sameMachine&&num_(s.qtyRound||s.qty_per_cycle)>0&&num_(s.minutesRound||s.minutes_per_cycle)>0; }).sort(function(a,b){return String(b.date||b.updated_at||"").localeCompare(String(a.date||a.updated_at||""));}).slice(0,10); if(matched.length){ const qtys=matched.map(function(s){return num_(s.qtyRound||s.qty_per_cycle);}).sort(function(a,b){return a-b;}); const mins=matched.map(function(s){return num_(s.minutesRound||s.minutes_per_cycle);}).sort(function(a,b){return a-b;}); const mid=function(a){const n=a.length;return n%2?a[(n-1)/2]:(a[n/2-1]+a[n/2])/2;}; r.cycle_output=mid(qtys);r.cycle_unit=matched[0].unit||matched[0].cycle_unit||"R";r.cycle_minutes=mid(mins); r.output_per_hour=r.cycle_minutes>0?r.cycle_output*60/r.cycle_minutes:0; }else{r.cycle_output=0;r.cycle_unit="";r.cycle_minutes=0;r.output_per_hour=0;} }); return {ok:true,version:"V84.4",action:"machinelearningsummary",rows:out,summary:{ history_rows:rows.length,learning_groups:out.length, high_confidence:out.filter(function(r){return r.status==="高信心建議";}).length, pending:out.filter(function(r){return r.status==="待累積";}).length },time:now_()}; } function refreshMachineLearning_(p) { p = p || {}; const summary = machineLearningSummary_({limit:1000,min_samples:1}); const sh = ensureSheet_(SHEET_MACHINE_LEARNING, MACHINE_LEARNING_HEADERS); clearDataKeepHeader_(sh, MACHINE_LEARNING_HEADERS); } /**************************************************** * V93.8 Auto Storage Manager ****************************************************/ const STORAGE_GOOGLE_LIMIT_ = 10000000; const STORAGE_WARN_PCT_ = 75; const STORAGE_TRIM_PCT_ = 80; const STORAGE_CRITICAL_PCT_ = 92; function storageHealthSummary_() { const d = inspectSpreadsheetStorage_(); const pct = Number(d.usage_pct || 0); let level = "ok"; let label = "正常"; } /**************************************************** * Sheet Helpers ****************************************************/ function readSheetRows_(sheetName) { const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName); if (!sh) return []; const range = sh.getDataRange(); const values = range.getValues(); if (!values || values.length <= 1) return []; const headers = values[0].map(function(h) { return String(h || "").trim(); }); const rows = []; for (let r = 1; r < values.length; r++) { const obj = {}; for (let c = 0; c < headers.length; c++) { const h = headers[c]; if (!h) continue; let v = values[r][c]; if (v instanceof Date) v = Utilities.formatDate(v, TZ, "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"); obj[h] = v; } const hasValue = Object.keys(obj).some(function(k) { return String(obj[k] || "").trim() !== ""; }); if (hasValue) rows.push(obj); } return rows; } function findSheetLoose_(ss, sheetName) { const wanted = String(sheetName || "").trim().toLowerCase(); if (!wanted) return null; // 先走官方精準查找。 let sh = ss.getSheetByName(String(sheetName || "").trim()); if (sh) return sh; // 再處理大小寫、前後空白或不可見空白造成的名稱差異。 const sheets = ss.getSheets(); for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; const cleanName = String(sheetName || "").trim(); const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock(); // 避免兩個 API 同時初始化同一張工作表而互相撞名。 lock.waitLock(15000); try { let sh = findSheetLoose_(ss, cleanName); if (!sh) { try { sh = ss.insertSheet(cleanName); } catch (err) { // 若另一個請求剛好已建立完成，重新查找並直接使用。 sh = findSheetLoose_(ss, cleanName); if (!sh) throw err; } } if (!Array.isArray(headers) || !headers.length) return sh; if (sh.getLastRow() === 0) { sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]); return sh; } const lastCol = Math.max(sh.getLastColumn(), headers.length); const current = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues()[0].map(function(v) { return String(v || "").trim(); }); const same = headers.every(function(h, i) { return current[i] === h; }); // 只修正表頭，不清除既有資料。 if (!same) sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]); return sh; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } /** * V93.6 儲存格安全工具 * Google Sheets 的 clearContents() 只清內容，不會釋放已配置的空白列與欄。 * 這組工具會在可重建資料表覆蓋／分批上傳時，先縮減舊網格，再按需要擴充。 */ function ensureSheetCapacity_(sh, requiredRows, requiredCols) { requiredRows = Math.max(1, Number(requiredRows || 1)); requiredCols = Math.max(1, Number(requiredCols || 1)); const maxRows = sh.getMaxRows(); const maxCols = sh.getMaxColumns(); if (maxRows < requiredRows) sh.insertRowsAfter(maxRows, requiredRows - maxRows); if (maxCols < requiredCols) sh.insertColumnsAfter(maxCols, requiredCols - maxCols); } function trimSheetGridSafe_(sh, keepRows, keepCols) { keepRows = Math.max(2, Number(keepRows || 2)); keepCols = Math.max(1, Number(keepCols || 1)); const maxRows = sh.getMaxRows(); const maxCols = sh.getMaxColumns(); if (maxRows > keepRows) sh.deleteRows(keepRows + 1, maxRows - keepRows); if (maxCols > keepCols) sh.deleteColumns(keepCols + 1, maxCols - keepCols); } function resetSheetForReplace_(sh, headers) { headers = Array.isArray(headers) && headers.length ? headers : ["value"]; sh.clearContents(); trimSheetGridSafe_(sh, 2, headers.length); ensureSheetCapacity_(sh, 2, headers.length); sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]); } function clearDataKeepHeader_(sh, headers) { resetSheetForReplace_(sh, headers); } function appendValues_(sh, values) { if (!values || !values.length) return; } function collectHeaders_(rows) { const set = {}; rows.forEach(function(r) { Object.keys(r || {}).forEach(function(k) { if (String(k || "").trim()) set[k] = true; }); }); const headers = Object.keys(set); } /**************************************************** * Maps / Statistics ****************************************************/ function buildEmployeeMap_(employees) { const map = {}; (employees || []).forEach(function(e) { const no = norm_(e.emp_no || e["工號"] || e["員工編號"] || ""); } /**************************************************** * Utility ****************************************************/ function outputJson_(obj, callback) { callback = String(callback || ""); if (callback) { return ContentService .createTextOutput(callback + "(" + JSON.stringify(obj) + ")") .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JAVASCRIPT); } return ContentService .createTextOutput(JSON.stringify(obj)) .setMimeType(ContentService.MimeType.JSON); } function now_() { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, "yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss"); } function today_() { return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), TZ, "yyyy-MM-dd"); } function dateKey_(v) { if (v instanceof Date) return Utilities.formatDate(v, TZ, "yyyy-MM-dd"); let s = String(v == null ? "" : v).trim(); if (!s) return ""; s = s.replace(/\//g, "-"); const m = s.match(/(\d{4})-(\d{1,2})-(\d{1,2})/); if (m) { return m[1] + "-" + String(m[2]).padStart(2, "0") + "-" + String(m[3]).padStart(2, "0"); } return s.slice(0, 10); } function norm_(v) { return String(v == null ? "" : v).trim().replace(/\s+/g, "").toUpperCase(); } function wo12_(v) { return norm_(v).slice(0, 12); } function num_(v) { const n = parseFloat(String(v == null ? "" : v).replace(/,/g, "")); return isNaN(n) ? 0 : n; } function pick_(obj, keys) { obj = obj || {}; for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) { const k = keys[i]; if (obj[k] !== undefined && obj[k] !== null && String(obj[k]).trim() !== "") return obj[k]; } return ""; } function isoWeekText_(v) { const d0 = parseDateOnly_(v); if (!d0) return ""; const d = new Date(Date.UTC(d0.getFullYear(), d0.getMonth(), d0.getDate())); const dayNum = d.getUTCDay() || 7; d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 4 - dayNum); const yearStart = new Date(Date.UTC(d.getUTCFullYear(), 0, 1)); const weekNo = Math.ceil((((d - yearStart) / 86400000) + 1) / 7); return d.getUTCFullYear() + "-W" + String(weekNo).padStart(2, "0"); } function parseDateOnly_(v) { if (v instanceof Date) return v; const s = dateKey_(v); const m = String(s || "").match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})/); if (!m) return null; return new Date(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3])); } // 若結構已標準，直接寫旗標，不再掃描或備份。 if (isTargetPlanSchemaStandardV912_()) { props.setProperty(TARGET_REPAIR_FLAG_V912, "OK"); return { ok: true, skipped: true, reason: "already_standard" }; } var lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); } var result = ensureTargetPlanSchemaV91_(); props.setProperty(TARGET_REPAIR_FLAG_V912, "OK"); return { ok: true, skipped: false, repaired: result && result.repaired ? result.repaired : 0, rows: result && result.rows ? result.rows : 0, backup_sheet: result && result.backup_sheet ? result.backup_sheet : "" }; } // 清單讀取不再觸發修復或等待鎖。 function listTargetPlansV91_(p, action) { p = p || {}; var rows = readSheetRows_(SHEET_TARGET); var start = dateKey_(p.start || ""); var end = dateKey_(p.end || ""); var exact = dateKey_(p.date || ""); } /**************************************************** * V93.4 Instant Shared Index Engine（旁路新增／不影響現行系統） * * 重要： * 1) 本模組不覆蓋 sharedDataLookup_，現有 APS／Target／Key In 繼續照常運作。 * 2) 先透過 sharedindexbuildstart + sharedindexbuildchunk 建立索引。 * 3) 驗證 sharedindexlookup 正確且快速後，後續版本才考慮切換。 ****************************************************/ const SHEET_SHARED_INDEX = "MES_Shared_Index"; const SHARED_INDEX_VERSION = "V93.4.1-INSTANT-HOTFIX"; const SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_WORKER = "sharedIndexAutoWorker_"; const SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_LIMIT = 500; const SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_RUNTIME_MS = 210000; const SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY = "MES_SHARED_INDEX_JOB_V934"; const SHARED_INDEX_HEADERS = [ "lookup_keys","source","source_row", "work_order_no","order_no","command_no","report_no","batch_no","part_no", "input_part_no","output_part_no","input_lot_no","output_lot_no", "customer","product_spec","process","machine", "target_qty","target_unit","plan_date","due_date","status","updated_at","indexed_at" ]; function sharedIndexSources_() { // V93.4：直接 ERP 來源優先，避免先掃 4～5 萬筆 source_data 才輪到 4-3／PD11B。 // Target_Order_Cache 與 source_data 仍完整保留，但排在直接來源之後。 return [ SHEET_43, SHEET_PD11B, SHEET_SL31A, SHEET_5C, SHEET_53, V78_SHEET_91, V78_SHEET_93, V78_SHEET_39, SHEET_TARGET_CACHE, SHEET_SOURCE ]; } function sharedIndexStatus_(p) { p = p || {}; const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_SHARED_INDEX); const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); let job = {}; try { job = JSON.parse(props.getProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY) || "{}"); } catch (ignore) {} const result = { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexstatus", index_sheet: SHEET_SHARED_INDEX, exists: !!sh, rows: sh ? Math.max(0, sh.getLastRow() - 1) : 0, columns: sh ? sh.getLastColumn() : 0, job: job, ready: !!(sh && sh.getLastRow() > 1 && job.status === "done" && job.version === SHARED_INDEX_VERSION), index_version: job.version || "", rebuild_required: !(job.status === "done" && job.version === SHARED_INDEX_VERSION), auto_trigger_active: sharedIndexHasAutoTrigger_(), progress: sharedIndexProgress_(job), current_time: now_() }; if (String(p.q || "").trim()) { const test = sharedIndexLookup_({ q: p.q, limit: p.limit || 20 }); result.test_lookup = { query: test.query, count: test.count, elapsed_ms: test.elapsed_ms }; } return result; } function sharedIndexBuildStart_(p) { p = p || {}; const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildstart", message:"索引正在由其他程序處理，請稍後再試" }; } try { sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); const sh = ensureSheet_(SHEET_SHARED_INDEX, SHARED_INDEX_HEADERS); clearDataKeepHeader_(sh, SHARED_INDEX_HEADERS); const sources = sharedIndexSources_(); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sourceInfo = sources.map(function(name) { const s = ss.getSheetByName(name); return { name: name, exists: !!s, rows: s ? Math.max(0, s.getLastRow() - 1) : 0 }; }); const job = { version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, status: "building", source_index: 0, source: sourceInfo.length ? sourceInfo[0].name : "", offset: 0, total_written: 0, total_read: 0, source_info: sourceInfo, started_at: now_(), updated_at: now_(), completed_at: "", auto_mode: false, auto_started_at: "", last_worker_at: "", last_error: "", run_count: 0 }; PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY, JSON.stringify(job)); return { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexbuildstart", message: "Shared Index 已初始化；可執行 sharedindexbuildauto 自動續跑，或使用 sharedindexbuildchunk 手動建立", job: job, time: now_() }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function sharedIndexBuildChunk_(p) { p = p || {}; const started = Date.now(); const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || 250), 20), 500); const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildchunk", message:"索引正在由其他程序處理，請稍後再試" }; } try { const props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties(); let job = {}; try { job = JSON.parse(props.getProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY) || "{}"); } catch (ignore) {} if (!job.status) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildchunk", message:"尚未開始建立索引，請先執行 sharedindexbuildstart" }; } if (job.status === "done") { return { ok:true, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildchunk", done:true, job:job, elapsed_ms:Date.now()-started }; } const sourceInfo = Array.isArray(job.source_info) ? job.source_info : []; let sourceIndex = Math.max(0, Number(job.source_index || 0)); let offset = Math.max(0, Number(job.offset || 0)); // 自動略過不存在或沒有資料的來源。 while (sourceIndex < sourceInfo.length && (!sourceInfo[sourceIndex].exists || Number(sourceInfo[sourceIndex].rows || 0) <= 0)) { sourceIndex++; offset = 0; } if (sourceIndex >= sourceInfo.length) { job.status = "done"; job.source_index = sourceIndex; job.source = ""; job.offset = 0; job.completed_at = now_(); job.updated_at = now_(); props.setProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY, JSON.stringify(job)); sharedIndexInvalidateCaches_(); sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); return { ok:true, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildchunk", done:true, job:job, elapsed_ms:Date.now()-started }; } const sourceName = sourceInfo[sourceIndex].name; const page = sharedReadSheetPage_(sourceName, offset, limit); const indexedAt = now_(); const out = []; page.rows.forEach(function(raw, idx) { // V93.2：來源欄名不一致時，除了標準欄位映射，也會從整列原始值擷取識別碼。 // 這可補足 4-3 等工作表中「命令單存在，但欄名未被 sharedNormalizeRow_ 辨識」的情況。 const n = sharedIndexNormalizeSourceRow_(raw, sourceName); const keys = sharedIndexKeys_(n, raw); if (!keys.length) return; out.push(sharedIndexOutputRow_(n, keys, sourceName, offset + idx + 2, indexedAt)); }); if (out.length) { const indexSheet = ensureSheet_(SHEET_SHARED_INDEX, SHARED_INDEX_HEADERS); appendValues_(indexSheet, out); } offset += page.rows.length; job.total_read = Number(job.total_read || 0) + page.rows.length; job.total_written = Number(job.total_written || 0) + out.length; if (page.rows.length === 0 || offset >= Number(page.total || 0)) { sourceIndex++; offset = 0; } // 下一來源若為空，下一次呼叫時自動略過。 job.source_index = sourceIndex; job.source = sourceIndex < sourceInfo.length ? sourceInfo[sourceIndex].name : ""; job.offset = offset; job.updated_at = now_(); if (sourceIndex >= sourceInfo.length) { job.status = "done"; job.source = ""; job.completed_at = now_(); sharedIndexInvalidateCaches_(); sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); } props.setProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY, JSON.stringify(job)); return { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexbuildchunk", source: sourceName, read: page.rows.length, written: out.length, done: job.status === "done", job: job, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started, time: now_() }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } /** * 自動建立入口： * - 沿用目前 building 工作，不清空已完成進度。 * - reset=1 時才重新初始化索引。 * - 單次 Web App 最多執行約 3.5 分鐘；未完成時建立每分鐘觸發器續跑。 * - 新索引仍為旁路，尚未接管 sharedlookup。 */ function sharedIndexBuildAuto_(p) { p = p || {}; const reset = String(p.reset || "") === "1" || String(p.reset || "").toLowerCase() === "true"; const limit = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_LIMIT), 50), 500); const maxMs = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.max_ms || SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_RUNTIME_MS), 30000), 240000); if (reset) { const started = sharedIndexBuildStart_({}); if (!started || started.ok === false) return started; } let job = sharedIndexReadJob_(); if (!job.status) { const started = sharedIndexBuildStart_({}); if (!started || started.ok === false) return started; job = started.job || sharedIndexReadJob_(); } if (job.status === "done") { sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); return { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexbuildauto", done: true, message: "Shared Index 已完成，不需重跑；需要重建請加 reset=1", job: job, progress: sharedIndexProgress_(job), time: now_() }; } job.auto_mode = true; job.auto_started_at = job.auto_started_at || now_(); job.last_error = ""; sharedIndexWriteJob_(job); const run = sharedIndexRunLoop_(maxMs, limit, "web"); job = sharedIndexReadJob_(); let trigger = { ok:true, active:false, message:"" }; if (job.status !== "done") { trigger = sharedIndexEnsureAutoTrigger_(); } else { sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); } return { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexbuildauto", done: job.status === "done", message: job.status === "done" ? "Shared Index 已自動建立完成" : "本次已處理一段進度，背景觸發器將自動續跑；可用 sharedindexstatus 查看進度", chunks: run.chunks, read: run.read, written: run.written, elapsed_ms: run.elapsed_ms, trigger: trigger, job: job, progress: sharedIndexProgress_(job), time: now_() }; } /** 時間觸發器呼叫的續跑函式。 */ function sharedIndexAutoWorker_() { const job = sharedIndexReadJob_(); if (!job.status || job.status === "done" || job.status === "stopped") { sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); return; } try { sharedIndexRunLoop_(SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_RUNTIME_MS, SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_LIMIT, "trigger"); const after = sharedIndexReadJob_(); if (after.status === "done") sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); } catch (err) { const failed = sharedIndexReadJob_(); failed.last_error = String(err && err.message ? err.message : err); failed.last_worker_at = now_(); failed.updated_at = now_(); sharedIndexWriteJob_(failed); // 保留觸發器，下一分鐘再嘗試；不影響現行 sharedlookup。 log_("SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_ERROR", failed.last_error); } } function sharedIndexRunLoop_(maxMs, limit, origin) { const started = Date.now(); let chunks = 0; let totalRead = 0; let totalWritten = 0; let last = null; while (Date.now() - started < maxMs) { const job = sharedIndexReadJob_(); if (!job.status || job.status === "done" || job.status === "stopped") break; last = sharedIndexBuildChunk_({ limit: limit }); if (!last || last.ok === false) { // 遇到其他程序持有鎖時，不視為永久失敗，留待下一次續跑。 break; } chunks++; totalRead += Number(last.read || 0); totalWritten += Number(last.written || 0); const updated = sharedIndexReadJob_(); updated.auto_mode = true; updated.last_worker_at = now_(); updated.last_worker_origin = origin || ""; updated.run_count = Number(updated.run_count || 0) + 1; updated.last_error = ""; sharedIndexWriteJob_(updated); if (last.done || updated.status === "done") break; Utilities.sleep(80); } return { chunks: chunks, read: totalRead, written: totalWritten, last: last, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started }; } function sharedIndexBuildStop_(p) { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildstop", message:"索引正在執行，請稍後再停止" }; } try { const job = sharedIndexReadJob_(); if (job.status && job.status !== "done") { job.status = "stopped"; job.updated_at = now_(); job.stopped_at = now_(); sharedIndexWriteJob_(job); } sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_(); return { ok:true, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexbuildstop", message:"Shared Index 自動續跑已停止；既有索引資料保留", job:job, time:now_() }; } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function sharedIndexReadJob_() { try { return JSON.parse(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY) || "{}"); } catch (ignore) { return {}; } } function sharedIndexWriteJob_(job) { PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(SHARED_INDEX_JOB_KEY, JSON.stringify(job || {})); return job; } function sharedIndexProgress_(job) { job = job || {}; const info = Array.isArray(job.source_info) ? job.source_info : []; const totalRows = info.reduce(function(sum, x) { return sum + Number(x && x.rows || 0); }, 0); const read = Number(job.total_read || 0); const pct = totalRows > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round(read / totalRows * 1000) / 10) : (job.status === "done" ? 100 : 0); return { status: job.status || "not_started", source: job.source || "", source_index: Number(job.source_index || 0), offset: Number(job.offset || 0), total_sources: info.length, total_rows: totalRows, total_read: read, total_written: Number(job.total_written || 0), percent: pct, last_worker_at: job.last_worker_at || "", last_error: job.last_error || "" }; } function sharedIndexEnsureAutoTrigger_() { try { if (sharedIndexHasAutoTrigger_()) { return { ok:true, active:true, created:false, message:"自動續跑觸發器已存在" }; } ScriptApp.newTrigger(SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_WORKER).timeBased().everyMinutes(1).create(); return { ok:true, active:true, created:true, message:"已建立每分鐘自動續跑觸發器" }; } catch (err) { return { ok:false, active:false, created:false, message:"無法建立背景觸發器；可再次開啟 sharedindexbuildauto 繼續：" + String(err && err.message ? err.message : err) }; } } function sharedIndexHasAutoTrigger_() { try { return ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers().some(function(t) { return t.getHandlerFunction() === SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_WORKER; }); } catch (ignore) { return false; } } function sharedIndexDeleteAutoTriggers_() { try { ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers().forEach(function(t) { if (t.getHandlerFunction() === SHARED_INDEX_AUTO_WORKER) ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t); }); } catch (ignore) {} } function sharedIndexLookup_(p) { p = p || {}; const started = Date.now(); const query = sharedNormalizeKey_(p.q || p.query || p.key || ""); const maxResults = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || 30), 1), 100); if (!query) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexlookup", message:"缺少查詢條件 q", rows:[] }; } const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_SHARED_INDEX); if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() <= 1) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexlookup", query:query, message:"MES_Shared_Index 尚未建立", count:0, rows:[], elapsed_ms:Date.now()-started }; } const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); const fingerprint = sharedIndexFingerprint_(); const cacheKey = "MES_SHARED_INDEX_LOOKUP_" + fingerprint + "_" + sharedCacheKeyToken_(query) + "_" + maxResults; const cached = cache.get(cacheKey); if (cached) { try { const obj = JSON.parse(cached); obj.cache_hit = true; obj.elapsed_ms = Date.now() - started; return obj; } catch (ignore) {} } const keyRange = sh.getRange(2, 1, sh.getLastRow() - 1, 1); const finder = keyRange.createTextFinder("|" + query + "|") .matchCase(false) .matchEntireCell(false) .useRegularExpression(false); const found = finder.findAll().slice(0, maxResults); const rows = found.map(function(cell) { const rowNo = cell.getRow(); const values = sh.getRange(rowNo, 1, 1, SHARED_INDEX_HEADERS.length).getValues()[0]; const obj = {}; SHARED_INDEX_HEADERS.forEach(function(h, i) { obj[h] = values[i]; }); return { source: obj.source || "", source_row: obj.source_row || "", work_order_no: obj.work_order_no || "", order_no: obj.order_no || "", command_no: obj.command_no || "", report_no: obj.report_no || "", batch_no: obj.batch_no || "", part_no: obj.part_no || "", input_part_no: obj.input_part_no || "", output_part_no: obj.output_part_no || "", input_lot_no: obj.input_lot_no || "", output_lot_no: obj.output_lot_no || "", customer: obj.customer || "", product_spec: obj.product_spec || "", process: obj.process || "", machine: obj.machine || "", target_qty: obj.target_qty || "", target_unit: obj.target_unit || "", plan_date: dateKey_(obj.plan_date || ""), due_date: dateKey_(obj.due_date || ""), status: obj.status || "", updated_at: obj.updated_at || "" }; }); // V93.4：索引尚未跑到該來源時，可即時從原始來源找到並寫入索引。 // 只影響 sharedindexlookup 測試 API；正式 sharedlookup 尚未切換，因此不會破壞現場系統。 const allowInstant = String(p.no_instant || "") !== "1" && String(p.instant || "1") !== "0"; if (!rows.length && allowInstant) { const instant = sharedIndexInstantFindAndUpsert_(query, maxResults); if (instant && instant.rows && instant.rows.length) { const instantResult = { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexlookup", engine: "V93.4 Instant Shared Index Engine", query: query, count: instant.rows.length, rows: instant.rows, instant_indexed: true, sources_searched: instant.sources_searched || [], fingerprint: sharedIndexFingerprint_(), cache_hit: false, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started, time: now_() }; sharedCachePutSafe_(cache, cacheKey, instantResult, 300); return instantResult; } } const result = { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexlookup", engine: "V93.4 Instant Shared Index Engine", query: query, count: rows.length, rows: rows, fingerprint: fingerprint, cache_hit: false, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started, time: now_() }; sharedCachePutSafe_(cache, cacheKey, result, 300); return result; } /** * V93.3 後台診斷 API（不出現在任何前端畫面） * 用法：?action=sharedindexdiagnose&q=MM2606020062 * 只讀取資料，不修改索引，也不影響正式 sharedlookup。 */ function sharedIndexDiagnose_(p) { p = p || {}; const started = Date.now(); const rawQuery = String(p.q || p.query || p.key || "").trim(); const query = sharedNormalizeKey_(rawQuery); const maxSources = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.max_sources || 10), 1), 10); const maxHitsPerSource = Math.min(Math.max(Number(p.limit || 5), 1), 20); if (!query) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexdiagnose", message:"缺少查詢條件 q" }; } const indexResult = sharedIndexLookup_({ q:query, limit:maxHitsPerSource }); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sources = sharedIndexSources_().slice(0, maxSources); const sourceHits = []; sources.forEach(function(sourceName) { const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sourceName); if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() <= 1 || sh.getLastColumn() <= 0) return; let cells = []; try { cells = sh.getDataRange().createTextFinder(rawQuery) .matchCase(false).matchEntireCell(false).useRegularExpression(false) .findAll().slice(0, maxHitsPerSource); } catch (err) { sourceHits.push({ source:sourceName, error:String(err && err.message ? err.message : err), hits:[] }); return; } const hits = cells.map(function(cell) { const rowNo = cell.getRow(); const colNo = cell.getColumn(); const lastCol = sh.getLastColumn(); const headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0]; const values = sh.getRange(rowNo, 1, 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0]; const raw = {}; headers.forEach(function(h, i) { raw[String(h || "COL_" + (i + 1)).trim()] = values[i]; }); const normalized = sharedIndexNormalizeSourceRow_(raw, sourceName); const keys = sharedIndexKeys_(normalized, raw); return { row: rowNo, column: colNo, header: headers[colNo - 1] || "", cell_value: values[colNo - 1] || "", normalized: { work_order_no: normalized.work_order_no || "", order_no: normalized.order_no || "", command_no: normalized.command_no || "", report_no: normalized.report_no || "", batch_no: normalized.batch_no || "", part_no: normalized.part_no || "" }, key_created: keys.indexOf(query) >= 0, matching_keys: keys.filter(function(k) { return k === query || k.indexOf(query) >= 0; }).slice(0, 20) }; }); if (hits.length) sourceHits.push({ source:sourceName, count:hits.length, hits:hits }); }); const rawFound = sourceHits.some(function(s) { return Array.isArray(s.hits) && s.hits.length > 0; }); const keyWouldBeCreated = sourceHits.some(function(s) { return (s.hits || []).some(function(h) { return h.key_created; }); }); return { ok: true, version: SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action: "sharedindexdiagnose", query: query, index: { found: Number(indexResult.count || 0) > 0, count: Number(indexResult.count || 0), elapsed_ms: Number(indexResult.elapsed_ms || 0) }, raw_source: { found: rawFound, key_would_be_created: keyWouldBeCreated, sources: sourceHits }, diagnosis: Number(indexResult.count || 0) > 0 ? } function sharedIndexInstantFindAndUpsert_(query, maxResults) { // V93.4.1 Hotfix：來源掃描不再等待背景 Builder 的 ScriptLock。 // 舊版在背景索引建立時會卡在 tryLock(8000)，最後回傳 sources_searched=[]、written=0。 // 現在先唯讀搜尋來源，只有真正 append 索引時才短暫取得寫入鎖。 const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sources = sharedIndexSources_(); const pending = []; const resultRows = []; const searched = []; const sourceStats = []; const seenSourceRows = {}; const indexedAt = now_(); for (let si = 0; si < sources.length && resultRows.length < maxResults; si++) { const sourceName = sources[si]; const sh = ss.getSheetByName(sourceName); if (!sh || sh.getLastRow() <= 1 || sh.getLastColumn() <= 0) { sourceStats.push({source:sourceName,exists:!!sh,hits:0,rows:0,skipped:true}); continue; } searched.push(sourceName); let cells = []; try { const exactLike = /^MM\d{10}$/.test(query) || /^\d{8,16}$/.test(query); const finder = sh.getDataRange().createTextFinder(query) .matchCase(false) .matchEntireCell(exactLike) .useRegularExpression(false); } const rowNos = []; cells.forEach(function(cell) { const r = cell.getRow(); if (r > 1 && rowNos.indexOf(r) < 0) rowNos.push(r); }); sourceStats.push({source:sourceName,exists:true,hits:cells.length,rows:rowNos.length,skipped:false}); if (!rowNos.length) continue; const lastCol = sh.getLastColumn(); const headers = sh.getRange(1,1,1,lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0]; for (let ri = 0; ri < rowNos.length && resultRows.length < maxResults; ri++) { const rowNo = rowNos[ri]; const unique = sourceName + "#" + rowNo; if (seenSourceRows[unique]) continue; seenSourceRows[unique] = true; const vals = sh.getRange(rowNo,1,1,lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0]; const raw = {}; headers.forEach(function(h,i){ raw[String(h || "COL_" + (i+1)).trim()] = vals[i]; }); const n = sharedIndexNormalizeSourceRow_(raw, sourceName); const keys = sharedIndexKeys_(n, raw); if (keys.indexOf(query) < 0) continue; pending.push(sharedIndexOutputRow_(n, keys, sourceName, rowNo, indexedAt)); resultRows.push(sharedIndexPublicRow_(n, sourceName, rowNo)); } } let written = 0; let writeBusy = false; if (pending.length) { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (lock.tryLock(5000)) { try { // 背景 Builder 可能在唯讀掃描期間已經寫入同一 Key；寫入前再確認一次。 const nowExisting = sharedIndexLookup_({q:query,limit:maxResults,no_instant:1}); } } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } else { // 查詢資料仍立即回傳；本次僅略過索引寫入，避免前端卡住。 writeBusy = true; } } return { rows:resultRows, written:written, sources_searched:searched, source_stats:sourceStats, write_busy:writeBusy, pending_count:pending.length }; } function sharedIndexOutputRow_(n, keys, sourceName, sourceRow, indexedAt) { n = n || {}; return [ "|" + keys.join("|") + "|", sourceName, sourceRow, n.work_order_no || "", n.order_no || "", n.command_no || "", n.report_no || "", n.batch_no || "", n.part_no || "", n.input_part_no || "", n.output_part_no || "", n.input_lot_no || "", n.output_lot_no || "", n.customer || "", n.product_spec || "", n.process || "", n.machine || "", n.target_qty !== undefined ? n.target_qty : "", n.target_unit || "", n.plan_date || "", n.due_date || "", n.status || "", n.updated_at || "", indexedAt || now_() ]; } function sharedIndexPublicRow_(n, sourceName, sourceRow) { n = n || {}; return { source:sourceName || n.source || "", source_row:sourceRow || "", work_order_no:n.work_order_no || "", order_no:n.order_no || "", command_no:n.command_no || "", report_no:n.report_no || "", batch_no:n.batch_no || "", part_no:n.part_no || "", input_part_no:n.input_part_no || "", output_part_no:n.output_part_no || "", input_lot_no:n.input_lot_no || "", output_lot_no:n.output_lot_no || "", customer:n.customer || "", product_spec:n.product_spec || "", process:n.process || "", machine:n.machine || "", target_qty:n.target_qty || "", target_unit:n.target_unit || "", plan_date:dateKey_(n.plan_date || ""), due_date:dateKey_(n.due_date || ""), status:n.status || "", updated_at:n.updated_at || "" }; } /** 後台健康檢查，不出現在任何正式頁面。 */ function sharedIndexHealth_(p) { p = p || {}; const started = Date.now(); const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(); const sh = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_SHARED_INDEX); } function sharedIndexClear_(p) { const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); if (!lock.tryLock(10000)) { return { ok:false, version:SHARED_INDEX_VERSION, action:"sharedindexclear", message:"索引正在由其他程序處理，請稍後再試" }; if (!useful) return; seen[k] = true; out.push(k); } function scanText(value, depth) { if (value === null || value === undefined || value === "") return; if (depth > 3) return; if (Array.isArray(value)) { value.forEach(function(v) { scanText(v, depth + 1); }); return; } if (typeof value === "object") { Object.keys(value).forEach(function(k) { scanText(value[k], depth + 1); }); return; } const text = String(value).trim(); if (!text) return; add(text); // 特別優先擷取正式 12 碼 MM 工單，不受前後 JSON、標點或欄位名稱影響。 const mmMatches = text.toUpperCase().match(/MM\d{10}/g) || []; } catch (ignore) {} } } scanText(raw, 0); return out; } function sharedIndexKeys_(n, raw) { n = n || {}; const vals = [ n.work_order_no, n.order_no, n.command_no, n.report_no, n.batch_no, n.part_no, n.input_part_no, n.output_part_no, n.input_lot_no, n.output_lot_no ]; } else { noCandidate++; conflictRows.push([ idx + 2, oldRaw, "", 0, resolution.matched_by.join(" | "), resolution.matched_values.join(" | "), resolution.reason || "沒有唯一可回推工單", v9931Now_() ]); } }); v995ReplaceData_(v995EnsureSheet_(ss, V995_INVALID_PATCH_SHEET, patchHeaders), patchHeaders, patchRows); v995ReplaceData_(v995EnsureSheet_(ss, V995_INVALID_CONFLICT_SHEET, conflictHeaders), conflictHeaders, conflictRows); return v995Result_(true, "INVALID_PREVIEW", { target_rows: t.values.length, valid_work_order_rows: validRows, invalid_work_order_rows: invalidRows, safe_patch_rows: patchRows.length, conflict_or_review_rows: conflictRows.length, no_candidate_rows: noCandidate, patch_sheet: V995_INVALID_PATCH_SHEET, conflict_sheet: V995_INVALID_CONFLICT_SHEET, elapsed_ms: Date.now() - started, message: "預覽完成；正式 Target_Order_Cache 尚未修改" }); } catch (e) { return v995Result_(false, "INVALID_PREVIEW", { message: v995Error_(e) }); } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function v995InvalidWorkOrderApply_(options) { options = options || {}; const lock = LockService.getScriptLock(); } catch (e) { return v995Result_(false, "INVALID_APPLY", { message: v995Error_(e) }); } finally { lock.releaseLock(); } } function v995MesHealthCheck_(options) { options = options || {}; const base = v994MesHealthCheck_(options); sources[wo]=sources[wo]||{}; if(rec.source_sheet) sources[wo][rec.source_sheet]=true; }); }); const ranked=Object.keys(scores).sort(function(a,b){ return scores[b]-scores[a]; }); if (!ranked.length) return {status:"NONE", matched_by:matchedBy, matched_values:matchedValues, reason:"現有識別碼無法在統一索引回推工單"}; if (safe) return { status:"SAFE", work_order_no:top, score:topScore, confidence: topScore>=10?"HIGH":"MEDIUM", matched_by:Object.keys(matched[top]||{}), matched_values:matchedValues, source_sheets:Object.keys(sources[top]||{}) }; } function v995SourceSheetNames_(ss) { const preferred = [ "source_data","DataHub_WorkOrder","SHEET_43","SHEET_PD11B","SHEET_SL31A", "V78_SHEET_91","V78_SHEET_93","V78_SHEET_39","SHEET_5C","SHEET_53", "4-3","PD11B","SL31A","9-1","9-3","3-9","5-C","5-3" ]; } function v995AddIndexKeys_(map, rec) { v995AddLookupKeys_(map, rec); } function v995AddLookupKeys_(map, rec) { [["order_no",rec.order_no],["command_no",rec.command_no],["daily_report_no",rec.daily_report_no], ["batch_no",rec.batch_no],["part_no",rec.part_no],["input_part_no",rec.input_part_no], ["output_part_no",rec.output_part_no]].forEach(function(x){ const k=v995Key_(x[1]); }); return r; } /**************************************************** * V101 APS AI Scheduler Core * 安全原則：Preview 寫入獨立工作表，不直接覆蓋 APS_Schedule。 * 排程優先：交期 → 急單 → 指定機台 → 換線 → 空檔 → 避免重疊。 ****************************************************/ const V101_VERSION = "V101.0-aps-ai-scheduler-core"; const V101_PREVIEW_SHEET = "V101_APS_Preview"; const V101_CONFLICT_SHEET = "V101_APS_Conflict"; const V101_STATE_KEY = "V101_APS_STATE"; const V101_BACKUP_PREFIX = "Backup_APS_Schedule_"; function v101ApsPreview_(p) { p = p || {};
